setIsListening(true);\n        speak(\"I'm listening. Search for products, filter by category, or say guide me.\");\n      } catch (e) {}\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Handle voice commands\n  const handleVoiceCommand = async (text: string) => {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    \n    // Search command\n    if (lower.includes('search') || lower.includes('find') || lower.includes('show me')) {\n      const searchTerms = lower.replace(/search|find|show me|for/g, '').trim();\n      setSearchQuery(searchTerms);\n      filterProducts(searchTerms, selectedCategory);\n      speak(`Searching for ${searchTerms}`);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Category filter\n    for (const cat of categories) {\n      if (lower.includes(cat.toLowerCase())) {\n        setSelectedCategory(cat);\n        filterProducts(searchQuery, cat);\n        speak(`Showing ${cat} products`);\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    if (lower.includes('all') || lower.includes('everything') || lower.includes('clear')) {\n      setSelectedCategory('all');\n      setSearchQuery('');\n      filterProducts('', 'all');\n      speak('Showing all products');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Guide command\n    if (lower.includes('guide') || lower.includes('tour') || lower.includes('walk')) {\n      setWalkerActive(true);\n      setWalkerIndex(0);\n      speak('Starting product tour. I\\'ll show you each product.');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Stop guide\n    if (lower.includes('stop') && walkerActive) {\n      setWalkerActive(false);\n      speak('Tour stopped.');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Semantic search\n    speak('Searching products...');\n    try {\n      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/products/search', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ query: text, limit: 20 })\n      });\n      const results = await response.json();\n      setFilteredProducts(results);\n      speak(`Found ${results.length} matching products`);\n    } catch (err) {\n      // Fallback to basic search\n      filterProducts(text, selectedCategory);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Filter products\n  const filterProducts = (query: string, category: string) => {\n    let filtered = products;\n    \n    if (category && category !== 'all') {\n      filtered = filtered.filter(p => p.category === category);\n    }\n    \n    if (query) {\n      const q = query.toLowerCase();\n      filtered = filtered.filter(p => \n        p.name.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||\n        p.description?.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||\n        p.sku?.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||\n        p.category?.toLowerCase().includes(q)\n      );\n    }\n    \n    setFilteredProducts(filtered);\n  };\n\n  // Walker effect\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!walkerActive || filteredProducts.length === 0) return;\n    \n    const interval = setInterval(() => {\n      setWalkerIndex(prev => {\n        const next = (prev + 1) % filteredProducts.length;\n        const product = filteredProducts[next];\n        speak(`${product.name}. ${product.price ? `$${product.price.toFixed(2)}` : ''}`);\n        \n        // Scroll to product\n        const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.product-card');\n        if (cards[next]) {\n          cards[next].scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });\n        }\n        \n        return next;\n      });\n    }, 4000);\n    \n    return () => clearInterval(interval);\n  }, Please contact the vendor.`;\n        }\n        else if (q.includes('dimension') || q.includes('size')) {\n            answer = product.dimensions\n                ? `The dimensions are ${product.dimensions}.`\n                : `Dimensions not specified. I can tell you about price, dimensions, SKU, or give you more details. Search for products, filter by category, or say guide me.\\\");\\n      } catch (e) {}\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Handle voice commands\\n  const handleVoiceCommand = async (text: string) => {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    \\n    // Search command\\n    if (lower.includes('search') || lower.includes('find') || lower.includes('show me')) {\\n      const searchTerms = lower.replace(/search|find|show me|for/g, '').trim();\\n      setSearchQuery(searchTerms);\\n      filterProducts(searchTerms, selectedCategory);\\n      speak(`Searching for ${searchTerms}`);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Category filter\\n    for (const cat of categories) {\\n      if (lower.includes(cat.toLowerCase())) {\\n        setSelectedCategory(cat);\\n        filterProducts(searchQuery, cat);\\n        speak(`Showing ${cat} products`);\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (lower.includes('all') || lower.includes('everything') || lower.includes('clear')) {\\n      setSelectedCategory('all');\\n      setSearchQuery('');\\n      filterProducts('', 'all');\\n      speak('Showing all products');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Guide command\\n    if (lower.includes('guide') || lower.includes('tour') || lower.includes('walk')) {\\n      setWalkerActive(true);\\n      setWalkerIndex(0);\\n      speak('Starting product tour. I\\\\'ll show you each product.');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Stop guide\\n    if (lower.includes('stop') && walkerActive) {\\n      setWalkerActive(false);\\n      speak('Tour stopped.');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Semantic search\\n    speak('Searching products...');\\n    try {\\n      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/products/search', {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({ query: text, limit: 20 })\\n      });\\n      const results = await response.json();\\n      setFilteredProducts(results);\\n      speak(`Found ${results.length} matching products`);\\n    } catch (err) {\\n      // Fallback to basic search\\n      filterProducts(text, selectedCategory);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Filter products\\n  const filterProducts = (query: string, category: string) => {\\n    let filtered = products;\\n    \\n    if (category && category !== 'all') {\\n      filtered = filtered.filter(p => p.category === category);\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (query) {\\n      const q = query.toLowerCase();\\n      filtered = filtered.filter(p => \\n        p.name.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||\\n        p.description?.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||\\n        p.sku?.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||\\n        p.category?.toLowerCase().includes(q)\\n      );\\n    }\\n    \\n    setFilteredProducts(filtered);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Walker effect\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!walkerActive || filteredProducts.length === 0) return;\\n    \\n    const interval = setInterval(() => {\\n      setWalkerIndex(prev => {\\n        const next = (prev + 1) % filteredProducts.length;\\n        const product = filteredProducts[next];\\n        speak(`${product.name}. ${product.price ? `$${product.price.toFixed(2)}` : ''}`);\\n        \\n        // Scroll to product\\n        const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.product-card');\\n        if (cards[next]) {\\n          cards[next].scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });\\n        }\\n        \\n        return next;\\n      });\\n    }, 4000);\\n    \\n    return () => clearInterval(interval);\\n  }, [walkerActive, filteredProducts]);\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div ref={containerRef} style={{\\n      minHeight: '100vh',\\n      background: 'linear-gradient(180deg, #0f172a 0%, #1e293b 100%)',\\n      padding: '20px'\\n    }}>\\n      {/* Header */}\\n      <div style={{\\n        maxWidth: 1400,\\n        margin: '0 auto 30px',\\n        display: 'flex',\\n        justifyContent: 'space-between',\\n        alignItems: 'center',\\n        flexWrap: 'wrap',\\n        gap: 20\\n      }}>\\n        <div>\\n          <h1 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '2em' }}>\\ud83d\\udecd\\ufe0f Product Catalog</h1>\\n          <p style={{ color: '#94a3b8', margin: '8px 0 0' }}>\\n            {filteredProducts.length} products \\u2022 Talk to any product for details\\n          </p>\\n        </div>\\n        \\n        {/* Search */}\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 10, alignItems: 'center' }}>\\n          <input\\n            type=\\\"text\\\"\\n            value={searchQuery}\\n            onChange={e => { setSearchQuery(e.target.value); filterProducts(e.target.value, selectedCategory); }}\\n            placeholder=\\\"Search products...\\\"\\n            style={{\\n              padding: '12px 20px',\\n              borderRadius: 25,\\n              border: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2)',\\n              background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n              color: '#fff',\\n              width: 250,\\n              outline: 'none'\\n            }}\\n          />\\n          \\n          <button\\n            onClick={toggleListening}\\n            style={{\\n              padding: '12px 20px',\\n              borderRadius: 25,\\n              border: 'none',\\n              background: isListening ? '#ef4444' : '#10b981',\\n              color: '#fff',\\n              fontWeight: 600,\\n              cursor: 'pointer',\\n              display: 'flex',\\n              alignItems: 'center',\\n              gap: 8\\n            }}\\n          >\\n            {isListening ? '\\u23f9\\ufe0f Stop' : '\\ud83c\\udfa4 Voice Search'}\\n          </button>\\n        </div>\\n      </div>\\n\\n      {/* Categories */}\\n      <div style={{\\n        maxWidth: 1400,\\n        margin: '0 auto 30px',\\n        display: 'flex',\\n        gap: 10,\\n        flexWrap: 'wrap'\\n      }}>\\n        <button\\n          onClick={() => { setSelectedCategory('all'); filterProducts(searchQuery, 'all'); }}\\n          style={{\\n            padding: '8px 20px',\\n            borderRadius: 20,\\n            border: 'none',\\n            background: selectedCategory === 'all' ? '#10b981' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\\n            color: selectedCategory === 'all' ? '#fff' : '#94a3b8',\\n            cursor: 'pointer'\\n          }}\\n        >\\n          All\\n        </button>\\n        {categories.map(cat => (\\n          <button\\n            key={cat}\\n            onClick={() => { setSelectedCategory(cat); filterProducts(searchQuery, cat); }}\\n            style={{\\n              padding: '8px 20px',\\n              borderRadius: 20,\\n              border: 'none',\\n              background: selectedCategory === cat ? '#10b981' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\\n              color: selectedCategory === cat ? '#fff' : '#94a3b8',\\n              cursor: 'pointer'\\n            }}\\n          >\\n            {cat}\\n          </button>\\n        ))}\\n        \\n        <button\\n          onClick={() => { setWalkerActive(!walkerActive); setWalkerIndex(0); }}\\n          style={{\\n            marginLeft: 'auto',\\n            padding: '8px 20px',\\n            borderRadius: 20,\\n            border: '1px solid #06b6d4',\\n            background: walkerActive ? 'rgba(6, 182, 212, 0.2)' : 'transparent',\\n            color: '#06b6d4',\\n            cursor: 'pointer',\\n            display: 'flex',\\n            alignItems: 'center',\\n            gap: 6\\n          }}\\n        >\\n          {walkerActive ? '\\u23f8\\ufe0f Stop Tour' : '\\ud83d\\udeb6 Product Tour'}\\n        </button>\\n      </div>\\n\\n      {/* Product Grid */}\\n      {isLoading ? (\\n        <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: 60 }}>\\n          <div style={{ fontSize: 40, marginBottom: 20 }}>\\u23f3</div>\\n          <p style={{ color: '#94a3b8' }}>Loading products...</p>\\n        </div>\\n      ) : filteredProducts.length === 0 ? (\\n        <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: 60 }}>\\n          <div style={{ fontSize: 40, marginBottom: 20 }}>\\ud83d\\udced</div>\\n          <p style={{ color: '#94a3b8' }}>No products found</p>\\n        </div>\\n      ) : (\\n        <div style={{\\n          maxWidth: 1400,\\n          margin: '0 auto',\\n          display: 'grid',\\n          gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fill, minmax(280px, 1fr))',\\n          gap: 24\\n        }}>\\n          {filteredProducts.map((product, idx) => (\\n            <div\\n              key={product.id}\\n              style={{\\n                transform: walkerActive && walkerIndex === idx ? 'scale(1.05)' : 'none',\\n                transition: 'transform 0.3s',\\n                position: 'relative'\\n              }}\\n            >\\n              {/* Walker indicator */}\\n              {walkerActive && walkerIndex === idx && (\\n                <div style={{\\n                  position: 'absolute',\\n                  top: -40,\\n                  left: '50%',\\n                  transform: 'translateX(-50%)',\\n                  fontSize: 30,\\n                  zIndex: 10,\\n                  animation: 'bounce 0.5s infinite'\\n                }}>\\n                  \\ud83d\\udc46\\n                </div>\\n              )}\\n              \\n              <ProductCard\\n                product={product}\\n                isWalkerActive={walkerActive && walkerIndex === idx}\\n              />\\n            </div>\\n          ))}\\n        </div>\\n      )}\\n\\n      {/* Floating AgenticBar */}\\n      <div style={{\\n        position: 'fixed',\\n        bottom: 20,\\n        left: '50%',\\n        transform: 'translateX(-50%)',\\n        background: 'rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.95)',\\n        borderRadius: 25,\\n        padding: '12px 24px',\\n        border: `2px solid ${isListening ? '#10b981' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'}`,\\n        boxShadow: '0 10px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)',\\n        display: 'flex',\\n        alignItems: 'center',\\n        gap: 16,\\n        backdropFilter: 'blur(10px)',\\n        zIndex: 1000\\n      }}>\\n        <div style={{\\n          width: 10,\\n          height: 10,\\n          borderRadius: '50%',\\n          background: isListening ? '#10b981' : '#64748b',\\n          animation: isListening ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none'\\n        }} />\\n        \\n        <span style={{ color: '#94a3b8', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\n          {isListening ? 'Listening...' : 'Voice Search Ready'}\\n        </span>\\n        \\n        {transcript && (\\n          <span style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', fontSize: '0.9em', maxWidth: 200, overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis', whiteSpace: 'nowrap' }}>\\n            \\\"{transcript}\\\"\\n          </span>\\n        )}\\n        \\n        {isListening && (\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 2 }}>\\n            {[...Array(5)].map((_, i) => (\\n              <div key={i} style={{\\n                width: 3,\\n                background: '#10b981',\\n                borderRadius: 1,\\n                animation: `wave 0.3s ease-in-out ${i * 0.05}s infinite alternate`,\\n                height: 10\\n              }} />\\n            ))}\\n          </div>\\n        )}\\n        \\n        <button\\n          onClick={toggleListening}\\n          style={{\\n            padding: '8px 16px',\\n            borderRadius: 20,\\n            border: 'none',\\n            background: isListening ? '#ef4444' : '#10b981',\\n            color: '#fff',\\n            fontWeight: 600,\\n            cursor: 'pointer'\\n          }}\\n        >\\n          {isListening ? '\\u23f9\\ufe0f' : '\\ud83c\\udfa4'}\\n        </button>\\n      </div>\\n\\n      <style>{`\\n        @keyframes pulse { 0%, 100% { opacity: 1; } 50% { opacity: 0.5; } }\\n        @keyframes wave { `}</style>\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default ProductCatalogPage;\\nCATALOGPAGE\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udd0c Creating product chat backend...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV/backend/product_chat_routes.cjs\\\" << 'PRODUCTCHAT'\\n// Product Chat Routes\\n// Talk to individual products\\n\\n// Chat with a specific product\\napp.post('/api/product-chat', async (req, res) => {\\n    try {\\n        const { productId, product, question } = req.body;\\n        \\n        // In (q.includes('price') || q.includes('cost') || q.includes('how much')) {\\n            answer = product.price \\n                ? `${product.name} is priced at $${product.price.toFixed(2)}.`\\n                : `Price information is not available. Please contact the vendor.`;\\n        }\\n        else if (q.includes('dimension') || q.includes('size')) {\\n            answer = product.dimensions\\n                ? `The dimensions are ${product.dimensions}.`\\n                : `Dimensions not specified. recognition.continuous = false;\n      recognition.interimResults = true;\n      \n      recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {\n        let text = '';\n        for (let i = 0; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n          text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\n        }\n        setTranscript(text);\n        \n        if (event.results[0].isFinal) {\n SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    u.rate = 0.95;\n    synthRef.current.speak(u);\n  }, []);\n\n  const toggleListening = () => {\n    if (isListening) {\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop();\n Contact agent for details.`;\n    }\n    else {\n      answer = `${property.title}. ${property.bedrooms ? `${property.bedrooms} beds` : ''} ${property.bathrooms ? `${property.bathrooms} baths` : ''} ${property.sqft ? `${property.sqft.toLocaleString()} sqft` : ''}. ${property.price ? `$${property.price.toLocaleString()}` : ''}. Create property\napp.post('/api/properties', async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n        const { title, description, price, address, city, state, bedrooms, bathrooms, sqft, property_type, listing_type,             RETURNING *`,\n            [title, description, price, address, city, state, bedrooms, bathrooms, sqft, property_type, listing_type, agent_id, builder_id, image_url]\n        );\n        \n        res.json({ success: true, property: result.rows[0] });\n    } catch (err) {\n        res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });\n    }\n});\n\n// Search properties with vector similarity\napp.post('/api/properties/search', async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n        const { query, listingType, minPrice, maxPrice, limit = 20 } = req.body;\n        \n        let sql = 'SELECT * FROM properties WHERE status = $1';\n        const params = ['active'];\n        let paramCount = 1;\n        \n        if (listingType) {\n            paramCount++;\n            sql += ` AND listing_type = $${paramCount}`;\n            params.push(listingType);\n        }\n        \n        if (minPrice) {\n            paramCount++;\n            sql += ` AND price >= $${paramCount}`;\n            params.push(minPrice);\n        }\n        \n        if (maxPrice) {\n            paramCount++;\n            sql += ` AND price <= $${paramCount}`;\n            params.push(maxPrice);\n        }\n        \n        // Text search\n        if (query) {\n            paramCount++;\n            sql += ` AND (title ILIKE $${paramCount} OR description ILIKE $${paramCount} OR address ILIKE $${paramCount} OR city ILIKE $${paramCount})`;\n            params.push(`%${query}%`);\n        }\n        \n        sql += ` ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT ${limit}`;\n        \n        const result = await pool.query(sql, params);\n        res.json(result.rows);\n    } catch (err) {\n        res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });\n    }\n});\n\nconsole.log('\u2705 Property routes req.body;\\n        \\n        let sql = 'SELECT * FROM properties WHERE status = $1';\\n        const params = ['active'];\\n        let paramCount = 1;\\n        \\n        if (listingType) {\\n            paramCount++;\\n            sql += ` AND listing_type = $${paramCount}`;\\n            params.push(listingType);\\n        }\\n        \\n        if (minPrice) {\\n            paramCount++;\\n $${paramCount}`;\\n            params.push(maxPrice);\\n        }\\n        \\n        // Text search\\n        if (query) {\\n            paramCount++;\\n            sql += ` AND (title ILIKE $${paramCount} OR description ILIKE $${paramCount} OR address ILIKE $${paramCount} OR city ILIKE $${paramCount})`;\\n            params.push(`%${query}%`);\\n        }\\n        \\n        sql += `
